CODEOWNERS infrastructure in Grafana is a comprehensive system for managing code ownership across the repository, tightly integrated with feature management.\\n\\nAt its core is the `.github/CODEOWNERS` file, which is the standard GitHub ownership definition used for pull request routing and review assignment. This file maps file patterns to GitHub teams and individuals using the format documented by GitHub.\\n\\nThe CODEOWNERS file is validated by a CI workflow (`.github/workflows/codeowners-validator.yml`) that runs on every pull request.
